Monophonic - A single note is played at a time with envelopes resetting between notes
Legato     - A single note is played at a time without envelopes resetting between notes

out /part[0,15]/polyType i Value of Synthesis polyphony type
Polyphonic - Each note is played independently
Monophonic - A single note is played at a time with envelopes resetting between notes
Legato     - A single note is played at a time without envelopes resetting between notes
